//----- Broadcast received events -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

WhenBroadcastReceived(GetStoredFile)
{
    Game File (.dot4) = Stored Game Files (.dot4)[File#];
}

WhenBroadcastReceived(Initialize)
{
    Call Initialize;
}

WhenBroadcastReceived(ResetData)
{
    Event.BroadcastAndWait("MIDI: Edit");
    Event.BroadcastAndWait("MIDI: Clear");
    Event.BroadcastAndWait("ClearMap");
    Event.BroadcastAndWait("ClearLevels");
    Legacy File (.dot3) = "";
    Music File (.midi) = "";
    Game File (.dot4) = "";
}
